[24/11/2024, 22:57:54] Subodh Dada: The error `Undefined array key 0` in the Laravel Voyager logs indicates an issue in Voyager's `SchemaManager` where it attempts to access an index in an array that doesn't exist. This typically happens when Voyager is trying to describe a table or access metadata for database columns but encounters unexpected data.

Here’s how to troubleshoot and resolve the issue:

---

### **1. Issue with Schema Manager in Voyager**

Voyager's `SchemaManager` is encountering a missing or improperly formatted index. This can occur due to:
- A missing primary key or unique key in the database table.
- Foreign key constraints that are not properly defined or removed.
- Mismatched or unsupported database schemas.

---

### **2. Verify Database Table Schema**

#### a. Ensure the `users` table has a **primary key**:
Run the following query in your database:
```sql
SHOW KEYS FROM users WHERE Key_name = 'PRIMARY';
```
- If the result is empty, add a primary key:
  ```sql
  ALTER TABLE users ADD PRIMARY KEY (id);
  ```

#### b. Check for unique constraints on the table:
Run:
```sql
SHOW INDEX FROM users;
```
Ensure there is a unique constraint on the `email` column, or create one:
```sql
ALTER TABLE users ADD UNIQUE (email);
```

#### c. Check for foreign keys:
Run:
```sql
SELECT TABLE_NAME, CONSTRAINT_NAME
FROM information_schema.KEY_COLUMN_USAGE
WHERE REFERENCED_TABLE_NAME = 'users';
```
Remove any foreign keys referencing the `users` table, if necessary:
```sql
ALTER TABLE table_name DROP FOREIGN KEY constraint_name;
```

---

### **3. Update Voyager’s Configuration**

#### a. Verify Voyager’s Bread Configurations
If you're editing the `users` table BREAD:
1. Go to **Tools > BREAD** in Voyager.
2. Ensure all fields are mapped correctly and all required fields (like `id`, `name`, `email`) are properly configured.

#### b. Enable or Reset Multilingual Configurations
If you're using multilingual features, ensure it’s properly enabled in the `config/voyager.php`:
```php
'multilingual' => [
    'enabled' => true, // or false if not used
    'default' => 'en',
    'locales' => ['en', 'ne'],
],
```

---

### **4. Update Laravel Voyager**
Ensure that your Laravel Voyager version is compatible with the Laravel version you are using.

- If you have access to Composer:
  ```bash
  composer update tcg/voyager
  ```

If not, manually update the Voyager package by uploading the latest version of Voyager to your `vendor/tcg/voyager` folder.

---

### **5. Patch SchemaManager**

If the issue persists, you can manually patch the `SchemaManager.php` file in Voyager:

#### Edit `vendor/tcg/voyager/src/Database/Schema/SchemaManager.php`:
Replace the problematic section at line 77:
```php
'key' => !empty($indexes) ? substr($indexes[0]['type'], 0, 3) : null,
```
With:
```php
'key' => isset($indexes[0]['type']) ? substr($indexes[0]['type'], 0, 3) : null,
```

This change adds a check to ensure the `type` key exists before attempting to access it.

---

### **6. Clear Cache**
After making changes, clear your Laravel cache:
- If you have access to Artisan:
  ```bash
  php artisan config:clear
  php artisan cache:clear
  ```
- If not, delete the `bootstrap/cache` files manually via FTP or your hosting panel.

---

### **7. Test Voyager**
Try accessing the Voyager database editor again. If the issue persists, it might be due to an unsupported Laravel version or an outdated Voyager package.

If you continue to face issues, share the output of:
```sql
SHOW CREATE TABLE users;
```
so I can verify your database schema against Voyager requirements.

[06/12/2024, 00:31:36] Subodh Dada: Hello,

As we announced in October, the Certification Authority (CA) for Apple Push Notification service (APNs) is changing. APNs will update the server certificates in sandbox on January 20, 2025, and in production on February 24, 2025. To continue using APNs without interruption, you’ll need to update your application’s Trust Store to include the new server certificate: SHA-2 Root : USERTrust RSA Certification Authority certificate.

To ensure a smooth transition and avoid push notification delivery failures, please make sure that both old and new server certificates are included in the Trust Store before the cut-off date for each of your application servers that connect to sandbox and production. At this time, you don’t need to update the APNs SSL provider certificates issued to you by Apple.

If you have any questions, please contact us.

The Apple Developer Relations Team

[13/12/2024, 17:32:35] Subodh Dada: ### PARTNERSHIP AGREEMENT

This Partnership Agreement ("Agreement") is made on this [Date] by and between:

1. **MEDICS Kathmandu Branch** (hereinafter referred to as "Kathmandu Branch"), located at [Address], and  
2. **Medico Network Pokhara** (hereinafter referred to as "Medico Network"), located at [Address].

**WHEREAS**  
- Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network wish to collaborate on the delivery of courses approved by the Council for Technical Education and Vocational Training (CTEVTE);  
- Both parties agree to share responsibilities, costs, and revenues as detailed in this Agreement to ensure the success of the courses delivered under this partnership.

NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants and promises herein contained, the parties agree as follows:

---

### 1. **Purpose of the Agreement**
This Agreement establishes a partnership between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network to deliver CTEVTE-approved courses through Medico Network’s center in Pokhara, with the ultimate goal of benefiting both parties and maximizing revenue.

---

### 2. **Revenue Sharing and Financial Responsibilities**
2.1 **Revenue Sharing**  
- After deducting the **teaching staff cost**, the net revenue generated from student fees will be shared equally (50% each) between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network.  
- Revenue sharing will be calculated only after the full fee payment or the total amount paid by each student.

2.2 **Marketing Costs**  
- A total of **20% of the generated revenue** will be allocated for course promotion and marketing.  
- This cost will be shared equally, with each party contributing 10% of the revenue toward the marketing budget.  
- Marketing funds must be used **exclusively to promote the agreed course(s) in Kathmandu**.  
- Both parties will maintain detailed records of marketing expenses, including where and how funds are spent. These records will be shared regularly to ensure full transparency.  
- Marketing plans and budgets must be reviewed and approved by both parties before implementation.

2.3 **Classroom Rental and Equipment**  
- The responsibility for classroom rental and **equipment purchases required for course delivery** under this partnership will rest solely with the Kathmandu Branch.  
- Medico Network **will not share the equipment costs** or contribute to classroom rentals when the courses are being conducted under Kathmandu Branch's name.

---

### 3. **Student Recruitment**
3.1 Both parties will collaborate to recruit students for the courses offered.  
3.2 The partnership will maintain transparency in tracking student payments to ensure accurate revenue sharing.

---

### 4. **Course Approvals and Future Collaborations**
4.1 Until Kathmandu Branch secures its own CTEVTE course approval, Medico Network’s existing course approval will be used for course delivery.  

4.2 Once the Kathmandu Branch obtains its CTEVTE approval:
   - Medico Network’s course approval will no longer be required for delivering courses under this partnership.
   - Students referred by Medico Network to Kathmandu Branch will be managed under **new terms** to be mutually agreed upon at that time.

4.3 In the future, when Kathmandu Branch secures approvals for UK-based courses, Medico Network will have the opportunity to deliver these courses under a franchising arrangement, with terms to be negotiated separately.

---

### 5. **Roles and Responsibilities**
5.1 **Kathmandu Branch Responsibilities**  
- Managing classroom rentals and equipment purchases for course delivery.  
- Handling marketing and promotions with the shared 20% marketing budget allocated for this purpose.  
- Ensuring timely payment to teaching staff.  
- Maintaining quality standards for course delivery in accordance with CTEVTE guidelines.

5.2 **Medico Network Responsibilities**  
- Using its CTEVTE approval to facilitate course delivery until Kathmandu Branch secures its own approval.  
- Collaborating on student recruitment and ensuring accurate reporting of fees collected from students.  
- Providing access to its center in Pokhara for the agreed courses.  
- Contributing 10% of the generated revenue to the shared marketing budget for course promotion in Kathmandu.

---

### 6. **Profit Distribution**
6.1 Profit calculations will be made **after deducting the teaching staff cost** and the allocated marketing budget from the total revenue.  
6.2 The remaining net revenue will be divided equally (50-50) between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network.  
6.3 Payments to both parties will be made no later than [Specific Date] following the receipt of full student payments.

---

### 7. **Duration and Termination**
7.1 This Agreement will remain in effect for an initial term of [Initial Term, e.g., 12 months] and may be extended upon mutual agreement.  
7.2 Either party may terminate the Agreement with [Notice Period, e.g., 60 days] written notice to the other party.  
7.3 In the event of termination, any ongoing courses will be completed under the agreed terms of this Agreement.

---

### 8. **Dispute Resolution**
8.1 Any disputes arising from this Agreement will be resolved through mutual discussions.  
8.2 If a resolution cannot be reached, the matter will be referred to arbitration under the laws of [Jurisdiction].

---

### 9. **Miscellaneous**
9.1 This Agreement constitutes the entire understanding between the parties and supersedes all prior agreements.  
9.2 Any amendments to this Agreement must be made in writing and signed by both parties.  
9.3 This Agreement shall be governed by the laws of [Jurisdiction].

---

**IN WITNESS WHEREOF**, the parties have executed this Agreement as of the date first written above.

[13/12/2024, 23:19:19] Subodh Dada: PARTNERSHIP AGREEMENT

This Partnership Agreement ("Agreement") is made on this [Date] by and between:

1. MEDICS Kathmandu Branch (hereinafter referred to as "Kathmandu Branch"), located at [Address], and


2. Medico Network Pokhara (hereinafter referred to as "Medico Network"), located at [Address].



WHEREAS

Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network wish to collaborate on the delivery of courses approved by the Council for Technical Education and Vocational Training (CTEVTE);

Kathmandu Branch intends to establish a separate, independent campus for additional cohorts under its own CTEVTE approval while maintaining the existing partnership with Medico Network to maximize revenue and expand reach.


NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants and promises herein contained, the parties agree as follows:


---

1. Purpose of the Agreement

This Agreement establishes a partnership between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network for the collaborative delivery of CTEVTE-approved courses at Medico Network’s center in Pokhara. Additionally, it outlines the framework for Kathmandu Branch to operate its own independent campus for separate cohorts while continuing to work cooperatively with Medico Network.


---

2. Revenue Sharing and Financial Responsibilities

2.1 Revenue Sharing

After deducting the teaching staff cost, the net revenue generated from student fees will be shared equally (50% each) between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network.

Revenue sharing will be calculated only after the full fee payment or the total amount paid by each student.


2.2 Marketing Costs

A total of 20% of the generated revenue will be allocated for course promotion and marketing.

This cost will be shared equally, with each party contributing 10% of the revenue toward the marketing budget.

Marketing funds must be used exclusively to promote the agreed course(s) in Kathmandu.

Both parties will maintain detailed records of marketing expenses, including where and how funds are spent. These records will be shared regularly to ensure full transparency.

Marketing plans and budgets must be reviewed and approved by both parties before implementation.


2.3 Classroom Rental and Equipment

The responsibility for classroom rental and equipment purchases required for course delivery under this partnership will rest solely with the Kathmandu Branch.

Medico Network will not share the equipment costs or contribute to classroom rentals when the courses are being conducted under Kathmandu Branch's name.



---

3. Student Recruitment

3.1 Both parties will collaborate to recruit students for the courses offered under this partnership.
3.2 The partnership will maintain transparency in tracking student payments to ensure accurate revenue sharing.
3.3 Students referred from Medico Network to the independent campus operated by Kathmandu Branch will be managed under terms to be negotiated separately.


---

4. Course Approvals and Dual-Cohort Operations

4.1 Existing Partnership Courses

Until Kathmandu Branch secures its own CTEVTE course approval, Medico Network’s existing course approval will be used for course delivery as part of this partnership.


4.2 New Independent Campus

Kathmandu Branch will establish an independent campus under its own CTEVTE approval, operating separately from this partnership.

Both campuses may run parallel cohorts to expand reach and revenue.


4.3 Student Referrals and Collaboration

Medico Network may refer students to the independent campus operated by Kathmandu Branch under new referral terms to be mutually agreed upon.

Both parties may collaborate on shared opportunities, including student referrals, dual-enrollment programs, and resource sharing, to maximize mutual benefits.


4.4 Future UK-Based Courses

Both parties will have the opportunity to offer UK-approved courses at their respective campuses.

Licensing terms and collaboration for these courses will be negotiated separately, ensuring both campuses benefit from expanded offerings.



---

5. Non-Competition Clause

To maintain goodwill and avoid direct competition:

Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network will not market or promote courses in a way that undermines the success of the other campus or cohort.

Both parties will focus on attracting students to their respective campuses based on their unique offerings and geographic reach.



---

6. Profit Distribution

6.1 Profit calculations for the partnership campus will be made after deducting the teaching staff cost and the allocated marketing budget from the total revenue.
6.2 The remaining net revenue will be divided equally (50-50) between the Kathmandu Branch and Medico Network.
6.3 Payments to both parties will be made no later than [Specific Date] following the receipt of full student payments.


---

7. Duration and Termination

7.1 This Agreement will remain in effect for an initial term of [Initial Term, e.g., 12 months] and may be extended upon mutual agreement.
7.2 Either party may terminate the Agreement with [Notice Period, e.g., 60 days] written notice to the other party.
7.3 In the event of termination, any ongoing courses will be completed under the agreed terms of this Agreement.


---

8. Dispute Resolution

8.1 Any disputes arising from this Agreement will be resolved through mutual discussions.
8.2 If a resolution cannot be reached, the matter will be referred to arbitration under the laws of [Jurisdiction].


---

9. Miscellaneous

9.1 This Agreement constitutes the entire understanding between the parties and supersedes all prior agreements.
9.2 Any amendments to this Agreement must be made in writing and signed by both parties.
9.3 This Agreement shall be governed by the laws of [Jurisdiction].


---

2. Dual-Cohort Strategy:

Kathmandu Branch will establish a separate, independent campus to run additional cohorts under its own CTEVTE approval.

Both campuses will operate parallel cohorts, expanding student intake and revenue.



3. Revenue Sharing:

Net revenue (after teaching staff costs) from the partnership campus will continue to be shared equally (50-50).



4. Marketing Costs:

A 20% marketing budget, split equally between both parties (10% each), will promote courses in Kathmandu.

Detailed records of marketing expenses will be maintained for transparency.



5. Independent Campus Operations:

Medico Network’s approval is not required for courses at the new campus.

Students referred by Medico Network to the new campus will be managed under separate referral terms to be mutually agreed.



6. Future UK-Based Courses:

Both campuses will have the opportunity to offer UK-approved courses, with licensing terms to be negotiated separately.



7. Non-Competition Assurance:

Both parties agree not to compete directly but will collaborate where beneficial, such as student referrals and resource sharing.

[17/01/2025, 16:09:31] Subodh Dada: Hello,


The issues we previously identified still need your attention.


If you have any questions, we are here to help. Reply to this message in App Store Connect and let us know.



Review Environment


Submission ID: c9258635-b193-489f-b63c-dd4412d67241

Review date: January 16, 2025

Version reviewed: 1.0


Guideline 2.5.4 - Performance - Software Requirements

We continue to find that the app declares support for location in the UIBackgroundModes key in your Info.plist file but we are unable to locate any features that require persistent location. Apps that declare support for location in the UIBackgroundModes key in your Info.plist file must have features that require persistent location.


Next Steps


If the app has a feature that requires persistent location, reply to this message and let us know how to locate this feature.


If the app does not require persistent real-time location updates, please remove the "location" setting from the UIBackgroundModes key. You may wish to use the significant-change location service or the region monitoring location service if persistent real-time location updates are not required for the app features.


Guideline 5.1.1(v) - Data Collection and Storage
Issue Description


We continue to find that the app supports account creation but does not include an option to initiate account deletion that meets all the requirements. The process for initiating account deletion must provide a consistent, transparent experience for users by meeting all of the following requirements:


- Allow users to complete account deletion without extra steps. Do not require them to create an additional account, register, or add a password to complete account deletion.

- Only offering to temporarily deactivate or disable an account is insufficient.

- If users need to visit a website to finish deleting their account, include a link directly to the website page where they can complete the process.

- The app may include confirmation steps to prevent users from accidentally deleting their account. However, only apps in highly-regulated industries may require users to use customer service resources, such as making a phone call or sending an email, to complete account deletion.


Next Steps


Update the app to include an account deletion option that fixes the following issues:


- The app requires users to send an email to initiate account deletion which is not appropriate.


If you believe the current account deletion option meets all the requirements, either because the app operates in a highly-regulated industry or for some other reason, reply to App Review in App Store Connect and provide additional information or documentation.


Support


- Reply to this message in your preferred language if you need assistance. If you need additional support, use the Contact Us module.

- Consult with fellow developers and Apple engineers on the Apple Developer Forums.

- Provide feedback on this message and your review experience by completing a short survey.
